name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n      typed_config:\n        \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n        grpc_service:\n          envoy_grpc:\n            cluster_name: ext-proc\n        route_cache_action: RETAIN  # Equivalent to disable_clear_route_cache: true\n```\n\n### 8.3 Load Testing\n\n```bash\n# Load test with timeout scenarios\n# Verify 504 responses under load\n# Verify deferred_close_timeout behavior with observability_mode\n\nwrk -t12 -c400 -d30s http://envoy:10000/test \\\n  --latency\n\n# Check response codes\n# HTTP 504 should appear in timeout scenarios\n```\n\n### 8.4 End-to-End Testing\n\n**Test Checklist:**\n- [ ] Ext_proc filter loads without errors\n- [ ] Request headers are sent to external processor\n- [ ] Response headers are properly processed\n- [ ] Route cache is cleared/retained per configuration\n- [ ] Timeout returns 504 (not 500)\n- [ ] Observability mode works with deferred_close_timeout\n- [ ] Multiple ext_proc filters in chain work correctly\n- [ ] Per-route overrides still work\n- [ ] Failure mode allows gracefully handles processor errors\n- [ ] Tracing shows correct parent-child relationships\n\n---\n\n## 9. Rollback Guidance\n\n### 9.1 Quick Rollback Procedure\n\nIf issues are detected post-upgrade:\n\n**Step 1: Revert Envoy Binary**\n```bash\n# Stop v1.31.0 Envoy\nsystemctl stop envoy\n\n# Restore v1.30.0 Envoy binary\ncp /path/to/envoy-v1.30.0 /usr/local/bin/envoy\n\n# Restart with old binary\nsystemctl start envoy\n```\n\n**Step 2: Revert Configuration** (if you updated configs)\n```bash\n# Restore v1.30.0 configs from backup\ncp /backup/envoy-config-v1.30.0.yaml /etc/envoy/envoy.yaml\n\n# Reload configuration\nenvoy-cli config reload\n```\n\n**Step 3: Verify Rollback**\n```bash\n# Check version\nenvoy --version  # Should show 1.30.0\n\n# Verify traffic is flowing\ncurl http://envoy:10000/health  # Should return 200\n\n# Monitor error codes\n# Should NOT see 504 responses\n# Should see 500 for ext_proc timeouts again\n```\n\n### 9.2 Known Issues and Workarounds\n\n#### Issue: 504 errors breaking downstream error handling\n\n**Symptom:** Client applications expecting 500 errors are not handling 504 correctly\n\n**Workaround 1: Custom Error Handler**\n```lua\n-- Add a Lua filter to convert 504 â†’ 500 if needed\n-- This is NOT recommended, just for emergency rollback\nif response.status_code == 504 then\n  response.status_code = 500\nend\n```\n\n**Workaround 2: Update Client Applications**\n- Update error handling to treat 504 same as 500\n- This is the correct long-term solution\n\n#### Issue: Route cache not being cleared/retained as expected\n\n**Symptom:** Route decisions aren't being recomputed correctly\n\n**Troubleshooting:**\n1. Verify `route_cache_action` is set correctly\n2. Check ext_proc logs for `clear_route_cache` value\n3. Verify the external processor is configured correctly\n4. Check if routes are actually being matched (use `debug` log level)\n\n**Workaround:** Explicitly set route_cache_action matching your intent:\n```yaml\n# Ensure explicit behavior\nroute_cache_action: DEFAULT  # or CLEAR or RETAIN\n```\n\n### 9.3 Version-Specific Support\n\n**v1.30.0:**\n- Oldest supported configuration format\n- Uses `disable_clear_route_cache` (boolean)\n- Returns 500 for ext_proc timeouts\n- No `deferred_close_timeout` support\n\n**v1.31.0:**\n- Current version (this migration guide)\n- Supports both `disable_clear_route_cache` and `route_cache_action`\n- Returns 504 for ext_proc timeouts\n- Supports `deferred_close_timeout`\n- Recommended migration target\n\n**v1.32.0+ (Future):**\n- Likely to deprecate `disable_clear_route_cache` further\n- Possible conversion to oneof fields\n- Monitor release notes for deprecation warnings\n\n---\n\n## 10. Compatibility Matrix\n\n### Supported Upgrade Paths\n\n| From Version | To Version | Compatibility | Config Changes |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| 1.30.0 | 1.31.0 | âś… Fully Compatible | Optional (backward compatible) |\n| 1.31.0 | 1.30.0 | âš ď¸Ź Requires rollback | Use `disable_clear_route_cache` instead of `route_cache_action` |\n\n### Configuration Compatibility\n\n| Feature | v1.30.0 | v1.31.0 |\n|---|---|---|\n| `disable_clear_route_cache` | âś… Supported | âś… Supported (deprecated) |\n| `route_cache_action` | âťŚ Not available | âś… Supported (recommended) |\n| `deferred_close_timeout` | âťŚ Not available | âś… Supported |\n| Error status 500 for timeout | âś… Default | âťŚ Changed to 504 |\n| Error status 504 for timeout | âťŚ Not used | âś… New default |\n| Tracing context in gRPC | âš ď¸Ź Not propagated | âś… Propagated |\n| `observability_mode` | âś… Supported | âś… Supported (improved) |\n\n---\n\n## 11. Performance Considerations\n\n### 11.1 Route Cache Behavior Impact\n\n**Potential Performance Changes:**\n\n- **CLEAR action:** May increase CPU usage due to frequent route recomputation\n  - Mitigated by: Route matching is optimized with trie structures\n  - Use case: Only when necessary for correctness\n\n- **RETAIN action:** May improve performance if routes are expensive to compute\n  - Ensure: External processor doesn't need to influence routing\n  - Trade-off: Less flexibility but faster path\n\n- **DEFAULT action:** Balanced approach, respects ext_proc decisions\n\n### 11.2 Deferred Close Timeout Impact\n\n- **Default 5s timeout:** Minimal overhead, suitable for most deployments\n- **Longer timeouts (10s+):** May hold more gRPC connections, slight memory increase\n- **Shorter timeouts (1s):** May result in premature stream closure if processor is slow\n- **Observability mode:** Adds minimal overhead when no processing is done\n\n### 11.3 Tracing Context Impact\n\n- **New in v1.31.0:** Minimal performance impact (header propagation)\n- **Benefit:** Improved observability for distributed tracing\n- **No tuning needed:** Works automatically\n\n---\n\n## 12. Common Migration Patterns\n\n### Pattern 1: Simple Authentication Service\n\n**Description:** External service that validates requests but doesn't modify routes\n\n```yaml\n# v1.30.0\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    grpc_service:\n      envoy_grpc:\n        cluster_name: auth-service\n    processing_mode:\n      request_header_mode: SEND\n    # Implicit DEFAULT: honor ext_proc's clear_route_cache\n```\n\n**Migration:** No changes needed; works as-is in v1.31.0\n\n### Pattern 2: Header Augmentation Service\n\n**Description:** External service that adds/modifies headers but doesn't need route recomputation\n\n```yaml\n# v1.30.0\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    grpc_service:\n      envoy_grpc:\n        cluster_name: header-service\n    processing_mode:\n      request_header_mode: SEND\n    disable_clear_route_cache: true\n```\n\n**Migration:**\n```yaml\n# v1.31.0 - Recommended update\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    grpc_service:\n      envoy_grpc:\n        cluster_name: header-service\n    processing_mode:\n      request_header_mode: SEND\n    route_cache_action: RETAIN  # Explicit intent: don't recompute routes\n```\n\n### Pattern 3: Logging/Observability Service\n\n**Description:** External service that only observes; no modification or routing changes\n\n```yaml\n# v1.30.0\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    grpc_service:\n      envoy_grpc:\n        cluster_name: logger\n    processing_mode:\n      request_header_mode: SEND\n    observability_mode: true\n    disable_clear_route_cache: true\n```\n\n**Migration:**\n```yaml\n# v1.31.0 - Enhanced configuration\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    grpc_service:\n      envoy_grpc:\n        cluster_name: logger\n    processing_mode:\n      request_header_mode: SEND\n    observability_mode: true\n    route_cache_action: RETAIN\n    # NEW: Control how long to keep stream for observations\n    deferred_close_timeout: \"10s\"  # Extended window for batch processing\n```\n\n### Pattern 4: Dynamic Routing Service\n\n**Description:** External service that makes routing decisions (NEW capability in v1.31.0)\n\n```yaml\n# v1.31.0 - Not possible in v1.30.0\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    grpc_service:\n      envoy_grpc:\n        cluster_name: routing-service\n    processing_mode:\n      request_header_mode: SEND\n    # NEW: Always recompute routes after external processor\n    route_cache_action: CLEAR\n    # Processor can modify headers to affect routing\n    mutation_rules:\n      allow_all_headers: false\n      allowed_headers:\n        patterns:\n        - exact: \"x-routing-decision\"\n```\n\n---\n\n## 13. FAQ\n\n**Q: Do I need to upgrade immediately?**\nA: No. v1.31.0 is fully backward compatible with v1.30.0 configurations. Upgrade at your convenience, but take advantage of new features like `route_cache_action` for clarity.\n\n**Q: Will my ext_proc filter break after upgrade?**\nA: No. All v1.30.0 configurations continue to work exactly as before. The 504 error code change is the only behavioral difference, which is semantically more correct.\n\n**Q: Can I downgrade from v1.31.0 to v1.30.0?**\nA: Yes, but you must remove `route_cache_action` and `deferred_close_timeout` fields if used. The core ext_proc functionality is identical.\n\n**Q: Should I update `disable_clear_route_cache` to `route_cache_action`?**\nA: Yes, eventually. It makes intent clearer and prepares for potential future deprecation. But it's not urgent since both work in v1.31.0.\n\n**Q: What if my clients depend on receiving 500 errors?**\nA: Update your clients to handle 504 the same way. This is the correct HTTP semantics for upstream timeouts. 504 actually provides better debugging information.\n\n**Q: Does observability_mode work differently in v1.31.0?**\nA: No, functionally identical. But the new `deferred_close_timeout` field allows better control over stream lifetime for batched observations.\n\n**Q: Will there be a v1.31.1 or hotfixes?**\nA: Check the official Envoy release schedule. Bug fixes are typically released as patch versions (1.31.1, 1.31.2, etc.).\n\n**Q: What about the grpc tracing context propagation?**\nA: This is automatic in v1.31.0. If you use OpenTelemetry or Jaeger tracing, ext_proc calls will now appear correctly in traces. No configuration needed.\n\n---\n\n## 14. Overview\n\nThis migration guide covers the upgrade path for the Envoy External Processing (ext_proc) HTTP filter from version 1.30.0 (April 2024) to version 1.31.0 (July 2024). The ext_proc filter enables external services to intercept and process HTTP traffic through a bidirectional gRPC stream.\n\nThe v1.31.0 release introduces several significant improvements to the ext_proc filter, including better control over route cache handling, enhanced error reporting, support for deferred stream closure in observability mode, and improved gRPC context propagation for tracing.\n\n**Key Headlines:**\n- New `route_cache_action` enum provides explicit control over route caching behavior\n- Timeout errors now return `504 Gateway Timeout` instead of `500 Internal Server Error`\n- Support for deferred stream closure timeout in observability mode\n- Enhanced tracing context propagation in gRPC bidirectional streams\n- Deprecation of `disable_clear_route_cache` boolean in favor of the new enum\n\n---\n\n## 2. Breaking Changes\n\n### 2.1 Route Cache Handling Redesign\n\n**Impact Level:** âš ď¸Ź **Moderate** - Requires configuration review and potential behavioral changes\n\nThe route cache clearing mechanism has been redesigned to use an explicit enum-based approach instead of a simple boolean flag.\n\n#### What Changed\n\n**v1.30.0 Configuration:**\n```protobuf\nmessage ExternalProcessor {\n  // Boolean flag to disable route cache clearing\n  bool disable_clear_route_cache = 11;\n}\n```\n\n**v1.31.0 Configuration:**\n```protobuf\nmessage ExternalProcessor {\n  // Enum-based route cache action (RECOMMENDED)\n  enum RouteCacheAction {\n    DEFAULT = 0;   // Clear only if ext_proc says so\n    CLEAR = 1;     // Always clear\n    RETAIN = 2;    // Never clear\n  }\n\n  RouteCacheAction route_cache_action = 18;\n\n  // Legacy boolean (still supported but marked for migration)\n  bool disable_clear_route_cache = 11\n      [(udpa.annotations.field_migrate).oneof_promotion = \"clear_route_cache_type\"];\n}\n```\n\n#### Migration Path\n\n**If you are currently using `disable_clear_route_cache: true`:**\n```yaml\n# v1.30.0 Configuration\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    disable_clear_route_cache: true  # Route cache is never cleared\n```\n\n**Upgrade to v1.31.0:**\n```yaml\n# v1.31.0 Configuration (RECOMMENDED)\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    route_cache_action: RETAIN  # Equivalent to disable_clear_route_cache: true\n```\n\n**If you are currently using the default behavior (`disable_clear_route_cache` not set):**\n```yaml\n# v1.30.0 Configuration (implicit DEFAULT behavior)\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    # disable_clear_route_cache not set means: clear on ext_proc request\n```\n\n**Upgrade to v1.31.0:**\n```yaml\n# v1.31.0 Configuration (RECOMMENDED)\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    route_cache_action: DEFAULT  # Clear only if ext_proc response says so\n```\n\n#### Behavior Comparison Table\n\n| Scenario | v1.30.0 Config | v1.31.0 Equivalent | Behavior |\n|----------|-----------------|-------------------|----------|\n| Default route cache handling | (not set) | `route_cache_action: DEFAULT` | Clear cache based on ext_proc response |\n| Never clear route cache | `disable_clear_route_cache: true` | `route_cache_action: RETAIN` | Never clear cache |\n| Always clear route cache | (not supported) | `route_cache_action: CLEAR` | **NEW:** Always clear cache regardless of ext_proc response |\n\n#### Implementation Details\n\n- **Source File:** `api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/ext_proc.proto` (lines 103-120)\n- **Proto Field:** `RouteCacheAction` enum with three values: DEFAULT (0), CLEAR (1), RETAIN (2)\n- **Deprecation Timeline:** The `disable_clear_route_cache` boolean will remain functional in v1.31.0 and subsequent releases, but using `route_cache_action` is strongly recommended\n\n#### Why This Change\n\nThe new enum-based approach provides three explicit states:\n1. **DEFAULT (0):** Follows ext_proc response directives - better for dynamic decision-making\n2. **CLEAR (1):** Always clears cache - useful for routes that require fresh decisions\n3. **RETAIN (2):** Never clears cache - useful for read-only operations or performance-sensitive paths\n\nThis is more explicit than the boolean approach and eliminates ambiguity around default behavior.\n\n---\n\n## 3. Deprecated Features\n\n### 3.1 `disable_clear_route_cache` Boolean Field\n\n**Status:** Deprecated (still functional in v1.31.0)\n\n**Deprecation Message:** Use `route_cache_action` enum instead\n\nThe `disable_clear_route_cache` boolean field is marked with UDPA deprecation annotation `field_migrate.oneof_promotion = \"clear_route_cache_type\"`, indicating it will eventually migrate to a oneof grouping.\n\n**Migration Advice:**\n1. Replace `disable_clear_route_cache: true` with `route_cache_action: RETAIN`\n2. Remove any explicit `disable_clear_route_cache: false` settings and use `route_cache_action: DEFAULT` instead\n3. Update any control plane configurations that generate ext_proc configs\n\n**Deprecation Timeline:**\n- v1.31.0: Both fields supported, both annotations present\n- v1.32.0+: Likely still supported, but planning should begin\n- Future: May be moved to oneof grouping or removed entirely\n\n---\n\n## 4. New Features\n\n### 4.1 Route Cache Action Enum\n\n**Status:** New - Stable and recommended\n\n**Proto Definition:**\n```protobuf\nmessage ExternalProcessor {\n  enum RouteCacheAction {\n    option (udpa.annotations.file_status).package_version_status = ACTIVE;\n\n    // Default behavior: clear route cache only when ext_proc response\n    // has clear_route_cache field set\n    DEFAULT = 0;\n\n    // Always clear the route cache when external processor responds\n    // with request headers, regardless of clear_route_cache setting\n    CLEAR = 1;\n\n    // Never clear the route cache, even if ext_proc sets clear_route_cache\n    // Equivalent to disable_clear_route_cache: true\n    RETAIN = 2;\n  }\n\n  RouteCacheAction route_cache_action = 18;\n}\n```\n\n**Use Cases:**\n\n**Case 1: Routes requiring fresh routing decisions**\n```yaml\n# Always recompute routes after ext_proc processing\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    route_cache_action: CLEAR\n```\n\n**Case 2: Routes where auth decisions determine routing**\n```yaml\n# External processor makes auth decisions that affect routing\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    route_cache_action: DEFAULT  # Honor ext_proc's clear_route_cache\n```\n\n**Case 3: Read-only observation mode**\n```yaml\n# External processor only observes, never changes routes\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    route_cache_action: RETAIN\n```\n\n### 4.2 Deferred Stream Closure Timeout\n\n**Status:** New - Specifically for observability_mode\n\n**Proto Definition:**\n```protobuf\nmessage ExternalProcessor {\n  // Specifies the deferred closure timeout for gRPC stream\n  // that connects to external processor. Currently, the deferred\n  // stream closure is only used in observability_mode.\n  //\n  // In observability mode, gRPC streams may be held open to the\n  // external processor longer than the lifetime of the regular client\n  // to backend stream. Envoy will eventually timeout the external\n  // processor stream according to this time limit.\n  //\n  // Default: 5000 milliseconds (5 seconds)\n  google.protobuf.Duration deferred_close_timeout = 19;\n}\n```\n\n**Use Cases:**\n\n**Example: Extended observability window**\n```yaml\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    observability_mode: true\n    # Keep the gRPC stream open for 30 seconds after the client disconnects\n    # to allow the external processor to continue observing\n    deferred_close_timeout: \"30s\"\n```\n\n**Important Notes:**\n- Only used when `observability_mode: true`\n- Default timeout is 5 seconds if not specified\n- The external processor can still close the stream before the timeout expires\n- This feature addresses flow control concerns and external processor buffering needs\n\n**Implementation:** `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.proto` (lines 260-265)\n\n### 4.3 Enhanced Error Handling\n\n**Status:** New - Minor behavioral change in error responses\n\nThe error handling for timeout scenarios has been improved to be more semantically correct.\n\n**Change:**\n- **v1.30.0:** Timeout errors return `500 Internal Server Error`\n- **v1.31.0:** Timeout errors return `504 Gateway Timeout`\n\n**Rationale:**\n- `504 Gateway Timeout` is semantically correct for upstream service timeouts\n- `500 Internal Server Error` incorrectly suggests an internal Envoy issue\n- This improves observability and makes client error handling more accurate\n\n**Affected Scenarios:**\n- External processor doesn't respond within `message_timeout`\n- External processor doesn't respond within `max_message_timeout`\n- In synchronous processing mode only (no timeout in async mode)\n\n**Configuration Example:**\n```yaml\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    grpc_service:\n      envoy_grpc:\n        cluster_name: ext-proc-cluster\n    # Set appropriate timeouts\n    message_timeout: \"200ms\"  # Default\n    max_message_timeout: \"1000ms\"  # Optional\n```\n\n**Migration Impact:**\n- If downstream clients depend on receiving `500` for ext_proc failures, they may need adjustment\n- Monitoring and alerting rules looking for `500` errors will no longer catch ext_proc timeouts\n- Update log aggregation and APM tools to monitor `504` for ext_proc failures\n\n---\n\n## 5. Configuration Updates\n\n### 5.1 Required Configuration Changes\n\nNone. All v1.30.0 configurations remain valid and functional in v1.31.0.\n\n### 5.2 Recommended Configuration Updates\n\n#### Update 1: Migrate from `disable_clear_route_cache` to `route_cache_action`\n\n**Before:**\n```yaml\nfilters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    grpc_service:\n      envoy_grpc:\n        cluster_name: ext-proc-cluster\n    processing_mode:\n      request_header_mode: SEND\n      response_header_mode: SEND\n    disable_clear_route_cache: true\n```\n\n**After:**\n```yaml\nfilters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    grpc_service:\n      envoy_grpc:\n        cluster_name: ext-proc-cluster\n    processing_mode:\n      request_header_mode: SEND\n      response_header_mode: SEND\n    # RECOMMENDED: Use explicit route cache action\n    route_cache_action: RETAIN  # or DEFAULT or CLEAR as appropriate\n```\n\n#### Update 2: Add Observability Mode Configuration (if using observability_mode)\n\n```yaml\nfilters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    grpc_service:\n      envoy_grpc:\n        cluster_name: ext-proc-cluster\n    observability_mode: true\n    # NEW: Control how long to keep the stream open for observations\n    deferred_close_timeout: \"5s\"  # 5 seconds (default)\n```\n\n### 5.3 Per-Route Configuration Updates\n\nNo changes required to per-route configurations. The `ExtProcPerRoute` and `ExtProcOverrides` messages remain unchanged.\n\n---\n\n## 6. Behavioral Changes\n\n### 6.1 Route Cache Action Default Behavior\n\n**Field:** `route_cache_action` (field 18)\n**Type:** `RouteCacheAction` enum\n**Default Value:** `DEFAULT` (0)\n\n**Behavior:**\n- When set to `DEFAULT`: The filter respects the `clear_route_cache` field in the external processor's response to request headers\n- When set to `CLEAR`: The filter always clears the route cache after external processing of request headers\n- When set to `RETAIN`: The filter never clears the route cache, even if the external processor requests it\n\n**Change from v1.30.0:**\n- v1.30.0 didn't have explicit CLEAR option; it was implicit in the default behavior\n- v1.30.0 had only two states via boolean: DEFAULT (route cache honored ext_proc) or RETAIN (never clear)\n\n### 6.2 Error Status Code Changes\n\n**Affected:** Timeout scenarios in ext_proc processing\n\n**Before (v1.30.0):**\n```\nHTTP/1.1 500 Internal Server Error\n```\n\n**After (v1.31.0):**\n```\nHTTP/1.1 504 Gateway Timeout\n```\n\n**When This Occurs:**\n- External processor doesn't respond before `message_timeout` expires\n- In synchronous processing mode (not observability_mode)\n- Only affects downstream error responses; upstream timeout handling unchanged\n\n**Impact Areas:**\n- Client-side error handling\n- Monitoring and alerting\n- Logs and tracing spans\n- Custom error pages/responses\n\n### 6.3 gRPC Tracing Context Propagation\n\n**Status:** Improved in v1.31.0\n\n**Change:** Tracing context headers are now properly propagated in bidirectional gRPC streams when using ext_proc.\n\n**Affected Clients:**\n- Envoy gRPC client (via `config.core.v3.GrpcService.envoy_grpc`)\n- Google C++ gRPC client (via `config.core.v3.GrpcService.google_grpc`)\n\n**Benefits:**\n- Distributed tracing works correctly with ext_proc\n- OpenTelemetry and Jaeger integrations improved\n- Better observability for ext_proc request/response timing\n\n**Configuration Impact:**\n- No changes needed; this works automatically\n- Tracing spans will now show correct parent-child relationships with ext_proc calls\n\n---\n\n## 7. Migration Steps\n\n### Step 1: Review Current Configuration\n\n```bash\n# Examine all ext_proc filter configurations\ngrep -r \"ext_proc\" /path/to/config\n\n# Check for uses of disable_clear_route_cache\ngrep -r \"disable_clear_route_cache\" /path/to/config\n```\n\n### Step 2: Plan Route Cache Migration\n\nFor each ext_proc filter configuration:\n\n| Current Setting | Migration Path | New Setting |\n|---|---|---|\n| `disable_clear_route_cache: true` | Keep as-is or upgrade | `route_cache_action: RETAIN` |\n| `disable_clear_route_cache: false` | Keep as-is or upgrade | Remove field, use implicit DEFAULT |\n| Not specified (implicit DEFAULT) | Keep as-is or upgrade | `route_cache_action: DEFAULT` |\n\n### Step 3: Update Monitoring and Alerting\n\nUpdate any monitoring rules that check for `500 Internal Server Error`:\n\n```yaml\n# OLD: Catch all 500 errors including ext_proc timeouts\n- alert: HighErrorRate\n  expr: rate(envoy_http_requests_total{response_code=\"500\"}[5m]) > 0.05\n\n# NEW: Separate concerns\n- alert: ExtProcTimeout\n  expr: rate(envoy_http_requests_total{response_code=\"504\"}[5m]) > 0.05\n- alert: OtherServerErrors\n  expr: rate(envoy_http_requests_total{response_code=\"500\"}[5m]) > 0.05\n```\n\n### Step 4: Update Logging and Analysis\n\nIf you have custom log parsing or analysis:\n\n```\n# v1.30.0 logs for ext_proc timeout\n[2024-04-15 10:23:45] ERROR ext_proc timeout -> HTTP 500\n\n# v1.31.0 logs for ext_proc timeout\n[2024-07-19 10:23:45] ERROR ext_proc timeout -> HTTP 504\n```\n\n### Step 5: Stage Deployment\n\n**Phase 1: Development/Staging**\n1. Deploy v1.31.0 Envoy binaries\n2. Keep all ext_proc configs unchanged (backward compatible)\n3. Verify ext_proc functionality with existing configs\n4. Test error handling with intentional timeouts\n\n**Phase 2: Production Canary**\n1. Route 5-10% of production traffic through v1.31.0\n2. Monitor error rates, latencies, and 504 vs 500 error distribution\n3. Verify that `504` errors are only ext_proc timeouts\n4. Validate downstream client error handling\n\n**Phase 3: Gradual Rollout**\n1. Gradually increase traffic through v1.31.0\n2. Update config for `route_cache_action` on non-critical routes\n3. Validate route caching behavior changes\n4. Monitor for any unexpected interactions\n\n**Phase 4: Update Configuration**\n1. Update all ext_proc configs to use `route_cache_action`\n2. Remove `disable_clear_route_cache` from configs\n3. Add `deferred_close_timeout` if using `observability_mode`\n4. Complete rollout to 100%\n\n### Step 6: Configuration Examples\n\n**Example 1: Basic Auth Service (DEFAULT route cache handling)**\n```yaml\n# Before\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    grpc_service:\n      envoy_grpc:\n        cluster_name: auth-processor\n    processing_mode:\n      request_header_mode: SEND\n\n# After (optional, uses default behavior)\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    grpc_service:\n      envoy_grpc:\n        cluster_name: auth-processor\n    processing_mode:\n      request_header_mode: SEND\n    route_cache_action: DEFAULT\n```\n\n**Example 2: Read-Only Logging Service (RETAIN route cache)**\n```yaml\n# Before\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    grpc_service:\n      envoy_grpc:\n        cluster_name: log-processor\n    disable_clear_route_cache: true\n    observability_mode: true\n\n# After\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    grpc_service:\n      envoy_grpc:\n        cluster_name: log-processor\n    route_cache_action: RETAIN\n    observability_mode: true\n    deferred_close_timeout: \"5s\"\n```\n\n**Example 3: Authorization Service with Dynamic Routes (CLEAR route cache)**\n```yaml\n# NEW in v1.31.0 - Not possible in v1.30.0\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    grpc_service:\n      envoy_grpc:\n        cluster_name: auth-processor\n    processing_mode:\n      request_header_mode: SEND\n      response_header_mode: SEND\n    # Always recompute routes after auth decisions\n    route_cache_action: CLEAR\n    # Modify headers based on auth outcome\n    mutation_rules:\n      allow_all_headers: false\n      allow_envoy_headers: false\n      allowed_headers:\n        patterns:\n        - exact: \"x-user-id\"\n        - exact: \"x-user-role\"\n```\n\n---\n\n## 8. Testing Recommendations\n\n### 8.1 Unit Testing\n\n**Test Case 1: Route Cache Action Behavior**\n```go\n// Test DEFAULT: cache cleared only if ext_proc says so\nfunc TestRouteCacheActionDefault() {\n    // Configure route_cache_action: DEFAULT\n    // Send ext_proc response with clear_route_cache: true\n    // Assert: route cache was cleared\n\n    // Send ext_proc response with clear_route_cache: false\n    // Assert: route cache was NOT cleared\n}\n\n// Test CLEAR: cache always cleared\nfunc TestRouteCacheActionClear() {\n    // Configure route_cache_action: CLEAR\n    // Send ext_proc response with clear_route_cache: false\n    // Assert: route cache was cleared anyway\n}\n\n// Test RETAIN: cache never cleared\nfunc TestRouteCacheActionRetain() {\n    // Configure route_cache_action: RETAIN\n    // Send ext_proc response with clear_route_cache: true\n    // Assert: route cache was NOT cleared\n}\n```\n\n**Test Case 2: Error Status Codes**\n```go\nfunc TestExtProcTimeoutReturns504() {\n    // Configure message_timeout: 100ms\n    // Don't respond from ext_proc\n    // Assert: Returns HTTP 504\n    // Assert: NOT HTTP 500\n}\n```\n\n### 8.2 Integration Testing\n\n**Test Scenario 1: Backward Compatibility**\n```yaml\n# v1.30.0 config should work unchanged in v1.31.0\n---\napiVersion: v1\nkind: ConfigMap\nmetadata:\n  name: envoy-config-v130\ndata:\n  envoy.yaml: |\n    http_filters:\n    - name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n      typed_config:\n        \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n        grpc_service:\n          envoy_grpc:\n            cluster_name: ext-proc\n        disable_clear_route_cache: true\n```\n\n**Test Scenario 2: Migration Validation**\n```yaml\n# Verify route_cache_action works as expected\n---\napiVersion: v1\nkind: ConfigMap\nmetadata:\n  name: envoy-config-v131\ndata:\n  envoy.yaml: |\n    http_filters:\n    - name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n      typed_config:\n        \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n        grpc_service:\n          envoy_grpc:\n            cluster_name: ext-proc\n        route_cache_action: RETAIN  # Equivalent to disable_clear_route_cache: true\n```\n\n### 8.3 Load Testing\n\n```bash\n# Load test with timeout scenarios\n# Verify 504 responses under load\n# Verify deferred_close_timeout behavior with observability_mode\n\nwrk -t12 -c400 -d30s http://envoy:10000/test \\\n  --latency\n\n# Check response codes\n# HTTP 504 should appear in timeout scenarios\n```\n\n### 8.4 End-to-End Testing\n\n**Test Checklist:**\n- [ ] Ext_proc filter loads without errors\n- [ ] Request headers are sent to external processor\n- [ ] Response headers are properly processed\n- [ ] Route cache is cleared/retained per configuration\n- [ ] Timeout returns 504 (not 500)\n- [ ] Observability mode works with deferred_close_timeout\n- [ ] Multiple ext_proc filters in chain work correctly\n- [ ] Per-route overrides still work\n- [ ] Failure mode allows gracefully handles processor errors\n- [ ] Tracing shows correct parent-child relationships\n\n---\n\n## 9. Rollback Guidance\n\n### 9.1 Quick Rollback Procedure\n\nIf issues are detected post-upgrade:\n\n**Step 1: Revert Envoy Binary**\n```bash\n# Stop v1.31.0 Envoy\nsystemctl stop envoy\n\n# Restore v1.30.0 Envoy binary\ncp /path/to/envoy-v1.30.0 /usr/local/bin/envoy\n\n# Restart with old binary\nsystemctl start envoy\n```\n\n**Step 2: Revert Configuration** (if you updated configs)\n```bash\n# Restore v1.30.0 configs from backup\ncp /backup/envoy-config-v1.30.0.yaml /etc/envoy/envoy.yaml\n\n# Reload configuration\nenvoy-cli config reload\n```\n\n**Step 3: Verify Rollback**\n```bash\n# Check version\nenvoy --version  # Should show 1.30.0\n\n# Verify traffic is flowing\ncurl http://envoy:10000/health  # Should return 200\n\n# Monitor error codes\n# Should NOT see 504 responses\n# Should see 500 for ext_proc timeouts again\n```\n\n### 9.2 Known Issues and Workarounds\n\n#### Issue: 504 errors breaking downstream error handling\n\n**Symptom:** Client applications expecting 500 errors are not handling 504 correctly\n\n**Workaround 1: Custom Error Handler**\n```lua\n-- Add a Lua filter to convert 504 â†’ 500 if needed\n-- This is NOT recommended, just for emergency rollback\nif response.status_code == 504 then\n  response.status_code = 500\nend\n```\n\n**Workaround 2: Update Client Applications**\n- Update error handling to treat 504 same as 500\n- This is the correct long-term solution\n\n#### Issue: Route cache not being cleared/retained as expected\n\n**Symptom:** Route decisions aren't being recomputed correctly\n\n**Troubleshooting:**\n1. Verify `route_cache_action` is set correctly\n2. Check ext_proc logs for `clear_route_cache` value\n3. Verify the external processor is configured correctly\n4. Check if routes are actually being matched (use `debug` log level)\n\n**Workaround:** Explicitly set route_cache_action matching your intent:\n```yaml\n# Ensure explicit behavior\nroute_cache_action: DEFAULT  # or CLEAR or RETAIN\n```\n\n### 9.3 Version-Specific Support\n\n**v1.30.0:**\n- Oldest supported configuration format\n- Uses `disable_clear_route_cache` (boolean)\n- Returns 500 for ext_proc timeouts\n- No `deferred_close_timeout` support\n\n**v1.31.0:**\n- Current version (this migration guide)\n- Supports both `disable_clear_route_cache` and `route_cache_action`\n- Returns 504 for ext_proc timeouts\n- Supports `deferred_close_timeout`\n- Recommended migration target\n\n**v1.32.0+ (Future):**\n- Likely to deprecate `disable_clear_route_cache` further\n- Possible conversion to oneof fields\n- Monitor release notes for deprecation warnings\n\n---\n\n## 10. Compatibility Matrix\n\n### Supported Upgrade Paths\n\n| From Version | To Version | Compatibility | Config Changes |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| 1.30.0 | 1.31.0 | âś… Fully Compatible | Optional (backward compatible) |\n| 1.31.0 | 1.30.0 | âš ď¸Ź Requires rollback | Use `disable_clear_route_cache` instead of `route_cache_action` |\n\n### Configuration Compatibility\n\n| Feature | v1.30.0 | v1.31.0 |\n|---|---|---|\n| `disable_clear_route_cache` | âś… Supported | âś… Supported (deprecated) |\n| `route_cache_action` | âťŚ Not available | âś… Supported (recommended) |\n| `deferred_close_timeout` | âťŚ Not available | âś… Supported |\n| Error status 500 for timeout | âś… Default | âťŚ Changed to 504 |\n| Error status 504 for timeout | âťŚ Not used | âś… New default |\n| Tracing context in gRPC | âš ď¸Ź Not propagated | âś… Propagated |\n| `observability_mode` | âś… Supported | âś… Supported (improved) |\n\n---\n\n## 11. Performance Considerations\n\n### 11.1 Route Cache Behavior Impact\n\n**Potential Performance Changes:**\n\n- **CLEAR action:** May increase CPU usage due to frequent route recomputation\n  - Mitigated by: Route matching is optimized with trie structures\n  - Use case: Only when necessary for correctness\n\n- **RETAIN action:** May improve performance if routes are expensive to compute\n  - Ensure: External processor doesn't need to influence routing\n  - Trade-off: Less flexibility but faster path\n\n- **DEFAULT action:** Balanced approach, respects ext_proc decisions\n\n### 11.2 Deferred Close Timeout Impact\n\n- **Default 5s timeout:** Minimal overhead, suitable for most deployments\n- **Longer timeouts (10s+):** May hold more gRPC connections, slight memory increase\n- **Shorter timeouts (1s):** May result in premature stream closure if processor is slow\n- **Observability mode:** Adds minimal overhead when no processing is done\n\n### 11.3 Tracing Context Impact\n\n- **New in v1.31.0:** Minimal performance impact (header propagation)\n- **Benefit:** Improved observability for distributed tracing\n- **No tuning needed:** Works automatically\n\n---\n\n## 12. Common Migration Patterns\n\n### Pattern 1: Simple Authentication Service\n\n**Description:** External service that validates requests but doesn't modify routes\n\n```yaml\n# v1.30.0\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    grpc_service:\n      envoy_grpc:\n        cluster_name: auth-service\n    processing_mode:\n      request_header_mode: SEND\n    # Implicit DEFAULT: honor ext_proc's clear_route_cache\n```\n\n**Migration:** No changes needed; works as-is in v1.31.0\n\n### Pattern 2: Header Augmentation Service\n\n**Description:** External service that adds/modifies headers but doesn't need route recomputation\n\n```yaml\n# v1.30.0\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    grpc_service:\n      envoy_grpc:\n        cluster_name: header-service\n    processing_mode:\n      request_header_mode: SEND\n    disable_clear_route_cache: true\n```\n\n**Migration:**\n```yaml\n# v1.31.0 - Recommended update\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    grpc_service:\n      envoy_grpc:\n        cluster_name: header-service\n    processing_mode:\n      request_header_mode: SEND\n    route_cache_action: RETAIN  # Explicit intent: don't recompute routes\n```\n\n### Pattern 3: Logging/Observability Service\n\n**Description:** External service that only observes; no modification or routing changes\n\n```yaml\n# v1.30.0\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    grpc_service:\n      envoy_grpc:\n        cluster_name: logger\n    processing_mode:\n      request_header_mode: SEND\n    observability_mode: true\n    disable_clear_route_cache: true\n```\n\n**Migration:**\n```yaml\n# v1.31.0 - Enhanced configuration\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    grpc_service:\n      envoy_grpc:\n        cluster_name: logger\n    processing_mode:\n      request_header_mode: SEND\n    observability_mode: true\n    route_cache_action: RETAIN\n    # NEW: Control how long to keep stream for observations\n    deferred_close_timeout: \"10s\"  # Extended window for batch processing\n```\n\n### Pattern 4: Dynamic Routing Service\n\n**Description:** External service that makes routing decisions (NEW capability in v1.31.0)\n\n```yaml\n# v1.31.0 - Not possible in v1.30.0\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    grpc_service:\n      envoy_grpc:\n        cluster_name: routing-service\n    processing_mode:\n      request_header_mode: SEND\n    # NEW: Always recompute routes after external processor\n    route_cache_action: CLEAR\n    # Processor can modify headers to affect routing\n    mutation_rules:\n      allow_all_headers: false\n      allowed_headers:\n        patterns:\n        - exact: \"x-routing-decision\"\n```\n\n---\n\n## 13. FAQ\n\n**Q: Do I need to upgrade immediately?**\nA: No. v1.31.0 is fully backward compatible with v1.30.0 configurations. Upgrade at your convenience, but take advantage of new features like `route_cache_action` for clarity.\n\n**Q: Will my ext_proc filter break after upgrade?**\nA: No. All v1.30.0 configurations continue to work exactly as before. The 504 error code change is the only behavioral difference, which is semantically more correct.\n\n**Q: Can I downgrade from v1.31.0 to v1.30.0?**\nA: Yes, but you must remove `route_cache_action` and `deferred_close_timeout` fields if used. The core ext_proc functionality is identical.\n\n**Q: Should I update `disable_clear_route_cache` to `route_cache_action`?**\nA: Yes, eventually. It makes intent clearer and prepares for potential future deprecation. But it's not urgent since both work in v1.31.0.\n\n**Q: What if my clients depend on receiving 500 errors?**\nA: Update your clients to handle 504 the same way. This is the correct HTTP semantics for upstream timeouts. 504 actually provides better debugging information.\n\n**Q: Does observability_mode work differently in v1.31.0?**\nA: No, functionally identical. But the new `deferred_close_timeout` field allows better control over stream lifetime for batched observations.\n\n**Q: Will there be a v1.31.1 or hotfixes?**\nA: Check the official Envoy release schedule. Bug fixes are typically released as patch versions (1.31.1, 1.31.2, etc.).\n\n**Q: What about the grpc tracing context propagation?**\nA: This is automatic in v1.31.0. If you use OpenTelemetry or Jaeger tracing, ext_proc calls will now appear correctly in traces. No configuration needed.\n\n---\n\n## 14.
